# View Specifications - Second Brain Platform

## Document Structure

Each view specification includes:
- **Purpose**: What the user accomplishes here
- **Route**: URL path
- **Layout**: ASCII wireframe
- **Components Used**: From VIEW-COMPONENTS.md
- **States**: Loading, empty, error, populated
- **Inner Views**: Panels, modals, sub-views
- **Actions**: What users can do
- **Responsive**: Mobile adaptations

---

# Core Views

## 1. Home Dashboard

### Purpose
First view after login. Shows system health, active work, and quick actions.

### Route
`/`

### Components Used
- `PageHeader` (with greeting)
- `RichTextInput` (quick chat)
- `AgentSelector` (dropdown)
- `AgentCard` (team grid)
- `EntityCard` + `ProgressBar` (workstreams)
- `MetricCard` (rituals, memories, goals, insights)
- `Timeline` (for activity feed variant)

### States

**Loading:**
- Skeleton cards for all sections
- Greeting still shows (from session)

**Empty (new user):**
- Onboarding wizard overlay
- "Create your first agent" CTA
- Sample workspace pre-populated

**Error:**
- Error banner at top
- Retry button
- Cached data shown if available

### Inner Views


### Components Used
- `PageHeader` (with back button)
- `ChatThread` (virtualized message list)
- `ChatMessage` (individual messages)
- `ToolCallCard` (collapsible tool displays)
- `ChatInput` (with attachments, voice, stop)

### States

**Streaming:**
- Animated cursor on assistant message
- Stop button visible
- Tool calls show progress

**Error:**
- Error message inline
- Retry button on message

### Inner Views

## 5. Agent Detail View

### Purpose

### Route
`/agents/:agentId`

## Summary

This document specifies **16 main views** plus:
- **20+ inner views** (panels, modals, sub-views)
- **Onboarding flow** (5 steps)
- **Global overlays** (command palette, shortcuts)
- **Responsive layouts** for mobile

Each view references components from `04-VIEW-COMPONENTS.md` for consistent implementation.
